9–32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on June 6, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/calderaro.jpg)
By Marc Calderaro











There were a lot of similar decks in the Top 8 this time around, but there’s more variety underneath. Here are all the people who finished below the Top 8, but above 33rd.







#### Mauricio Enrique Aguero Culligan's Green-White Tokens – GP Costa Rica, 9th


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
